---------------------
CREATE TABLE `cat_contact_type` (
  `id_contact_type` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `contact_type` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id_contact_type`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_spanish_ci;


--  - - - - - - 
SELECT 
p.id_package,
p.phone,
p.tracking,
ct.contact_type  
FROM package p
INNER JOIN cat_contact c ON c.phone=p.phone 
INNER JOIN cat_contact_type ct ON ct.id_contact_type =c.id_contact_type 
WHERE  1 
AND p.id_location IN(1) 
AND p.id_status IN(1)
AND ct.id_contact_type IN(1)
ORDER BY p.phone ASC
;


SELECT 
p.phone,
GROUP_CONCAT(tracking) AS trackings
FROM package p
INNER JOIN cat_contact c ON c.phone=p.phone 
INNER JOIN cat_contact_type ct ON ct.id_contact_type =c.id_contact_type 
WHERE  1 
AND p.id_location IN(1) 
AND p.id_status IN(1)
AND ct.id_contact_type IN(1)
GROUP BY p.phone
ORDER BY p.phone ASC
;
-- ------------------
SELECT 
    p.phone,
    (SELECT cc.contact_name FROM cat_contact cc WHERE cc.phone = c.phone LIMIT 1) AS contact_name,
    COUNT(p.tracking) AS total_trackings,
    GROUP_CONCAT(p.tracking) AS trackings
FROM package p
INNER JOIN cat_contact c ON c.phone = p.phone 
INNER JOIN cat_contact_type ct ON ct.id_contact_type = c.id_contact_type 
WHERE  
    p.id_location IN (1) 
    AND p.id_status IN (1)
    AND ct.id_contact_type IN (1)
GROUP BY p.phone, c.phone
ORDER BY p.phone ASC;

SELECT 
p.id_package,
	p.phone,
	p.receiver,
	cc.contact_name phone2
FROM package p
inner join cat_contact cc on cc.phone=p.phone and cc.contact_name=p.receiver
WHERE 
	p.id_location IN (1) 
	AND p.id_status IN (1) 
ORDER BY p.phone ASC
;

select * from cat_contact where phone in(7771885284);

SELECT 
	p.phone,
	COUNT(p.tracking) AS total_p,
	if((SELECT count(cc.contact_name) FROM cat_contact cc WHERE cc.phone = c.phone)=1,
		(SELECT cc.contact_name FROM cat_contact cc WHERE cc.phone = c.phone),
		concat((SELECT cc.contact_name FROM cat_contact cc WHERE cc.phone = c.phone limit 1),'+',(SELECT count(cc.contact_name) FROM cat_contact cc WHERE cc.phone = c.phone)-1)
	) as main_name,
	GROUP_CONCAT(p.receiver) AS list_names,
	GROUP_CONCAT(p.tracking) AS trackings,
	GROUP_CONCAT(p.id_package) AS ids 
FROM package p 
INNER JOIN cat_contact c ON c.phone=p.phone AND c.contact_name=p.receiver 
INNER JOIN cat_contact_type ct ON ct.id_contact_type = c.id_contact_type 
WHERE 
	p.id_location IN (1) 
	AND p.id_status IN (1) 
	AND ct.id_contact_type IN (1) 
	GROUP BY p.phone,main_name  
	ORDER BY p.phone ASC
;

SELECT 
			p.phone,
			p.receiver contact_name,
			COUNT(p.tracking) AS total_p,
			GROUP_CONCAT(p.tracking) AS trackings,
			GROUP_CONCAT(p.id_package) AS ids 
			FROM package p 
			INNER JOIN cat_contact c ON c.phone=p.phone
			INNER JOIN cat_contact_type ct ON ct.id_contact_type = c.id_contact_type 
			WHERE 
			p.id_location IN (1) 
			AND p.id_status IN (1) 
			AND ct.id_contact_type IN (1) 
			GROUP BY p.phone,p.receiver  
			ORDER BY p.phone asc;

---------------------
CREATE TABLE `cat_contact_type` (
  `id_contact_type` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `contact_type` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8_spanish_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id_contact_type`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_spanish_ci;


--  - - - - - - 
SELECT 
p.id_package,
p.phone,
p.tracking,
ct.contact_type  
FROM package p
INNER JOIN cat_contact c ON c.phone=p.phone 
INNER JOIN cat_contact_type ct ON ct.id_contact_type =c.id_contact_type 
WHERE  1 
AND p.id_location IN(1) 
AND p.id_status IN(1)
AND ct.id_contact_type IN(1)
ORDER BY p.phone ASC
;


SELECT 
p.phone,
GROUP_CONCAT(tracking) AS trackings
FROM package p
INNER JOIN cat_contact c ON c.phone=p.phone 
INNER JOIN cat_contact_type ct ON ct.id_contact_type =c.id_contact_type 
WHERE  1 
AND p.id_location IN(1) 
AND p.id_status IN(1)
AND ct.id_contact_type IN(1)
GROUP BY p.phone
ORDER BY p.phone ASC
;
-- ------------------
SELECT 
    p.phone,
    (SELECT cc.contact_name FROM cat_contact cc WHERE cc.phone = c.phone LIMIT 1) AS contact_name,
    COUNT(p.tracking) AS total_trackings,
    GROUP_CONCAT(p.tracking) AS trackings
FROM package p
INNER JOIN cat_contact c ON c.phone = p.phone 
INNER JOIN cat_contact_type ct ON ct.id_contact_type = c.id_contact_type 
WHERE  
    p.id_location IN (1) 
    AND p.id_status IN (1)
    AND ct.id_contact_type IN (1)
GROUP BY p.phone, c.phone
ORDER BY p.phone ASC;
